Input by Yoshiyasu Yonezawa et al. 
(Institute for Comprehensive Studies of Buddhism, Taisho University)

Revised reference system:

*Vin_n.       = vastu
**(Vin_n,n,n) = vastu,chapter,section
Vin_n.n       = vastu.line

[nn] = fol. no.
